#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query+ (sql_dp_prod_we)

- **Achivement in % **

  ```
  IF  [Gross deposit + Cashout achivement ]/SUM([Target ])>1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE  [Gross deposit + Cashout achivement ]/SUM([Target ]) END
  ```

- **Actual Cashout**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' THEN [Diamond Cashout] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN [Platinum Plus Cashout] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Deposit**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' THEN [Diamond Deposit] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN [Platinum Plus Deposit] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **AO Achievement**

  ```
  IF  [AO Actual Ratio]<[AO Portfolio benchmark] THEN 0.25
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/[AO Target]>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-[AO Portfolio benchmark])/([AO Target]-[AO Portfolio benchmark])+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-[AO Portfolio benchmark])/([AO Target]-[AO Portfolio benchmark])+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

- **AO Diamond **

  ```
  { FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) }
  ```

- **AO Diamond Ratio (copy)**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: AVG(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN [AO Diamond ]/[EOM Diamond] END) }
  ```

- **AO Platinum Plus **

  ```
  { FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF  [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) }
  ```

- **AO Portfolio benchmark**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

- **AO Portfolio benchmark (copy)**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)]THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

- **AO Ratio AVG 6 Months**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: AVG(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN (([AO Diamond ]/[EOM Diamond])*1 + ([AO Platinum Plus ]/[EOM Platinum Plus])*9)/10 END) }
  ```

- **AO Ratio AVG 6 Months (copy)**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: AVG(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] THEN (([AO Diamond ]/[EOM Diamond])*1 + ([AO Platinum Plus ]/[EOM Platinum Plus])*9)/10 END) }
  ```

- **AO Target**

  ```
  [AO Portfolio benchmark] * 1.06
  ```

- **Calculation1**

  ```
  {FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Cashout]END)}
  ```

- **Calculation2**

  ```
  {FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Deposit] END)}
  ```

- **Calculation3**

  ```
  sum ({ FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Cashout] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Deposit] END) })
  ```

- **Cash out ratio achievement **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: AVG(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] AND  [region] = 'UK - Diamond' THEN [Diamond Deposit]
  ELSEIF  DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] AND  [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN [Platinum Plus Deposit]
  ELSEIF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth] END) }
  ```

- **Cash out ratio benchmark **

  ```
  {FIXED [region],[type_of_kpi]: [Cash out ratio benchmark  (copy)]   }
  ```

- **Cash out ratio benchmark  (copy)**

  ```
  if SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club],[ActiveDate],[AccountManager]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN [Total Cashout  ]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club],[ActiveDate],[AccountManager]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN [Total Deposit ]  END) })>0.9 THEN 0.9 ELSE
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club],[ActiveDate],[AccountManager]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN [Total Cashout  ]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club],[ActiveDate],[AccountManager]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN [Total Deposit ]  END) }) END
  ```

- **Cashout ratio achievement **

  ```
  IF (sum ({ FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Cashout] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Deposit] END) }))>1 THEN 1 
  ELSE (sum ({ FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Cashout] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Actual Deposit] END) })) END
  ```

- **Diamond Cashout**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] AND  [Club] = 'Diamond' THEN [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth] END) }
  ```

- **Diamond Deposit**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] AND  [Club] = 'Diamond' THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth] END) }
  ```

- **EOM Diamond**

  ```
  { FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF  [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }
  ```

- **EOM Platinum Plus**

  ```
  { FIXED [account_manager],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club] in ('Platinum Plus') THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }
  ```

- **Gross deposit + Cashout achivement **

  ```
  (SUM([Actual Deposit])*(SUM([Cash out ratio benchmark ])-([Cashout ratio achievement ])))+SUM([Actual Deposit])
  ```

- **High Tier AO Ratio **

  ```
  ([Ratio AO Diamond]*1+[Ratio AO Platinum Plus]*9)/10
  ```

- **Platinum Plus Cashout**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] AND  [Club] = 'Platinum Plus' THEN [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth] END) }
  ```

- **Platinum Plus Deposit**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate] AND  [Club] = 'Platinum Plus' THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth] END) }
  ```

- **Ratio AO Diamond**

  ```
  SUM([AO Diamond ])/SUM([EOM Diamond])
  ```

- **Ratio AO Platinum Plus**

  ```
  SUM([AO Platinum Plus ])/SUM([EOM Platinum Plus])
  ```

- **Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX([target]) }
  ```

- **Target  (copy)**

  ```
  { FIXED [account_manager],[Date],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2)] and [EOM_Club] in ('Diamond') THEN [Total_In_Club] END) }
  ```

- **Total Cashout  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club],[ActiveDate]: MAX( [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth]) }
  ```

- **Total Deposit **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[account_manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club],[ActiveDate]: MAX( [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth]) }
  ```

### Workbook: Account Manager Targets 2025

#### Datasource: All KPIs

- ** Deposit Calculation**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: 
     MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND 
             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') 
         THEN [Actual Deposit+IBAN ]
     END) 
  }
  ```

- **%Achievement Trigger**

  ```
  (COUNTD([Id])-COUNTD([Expierd]))/COUNTD([Id])
  ```

- **Achievement in % **

  ```
  IF  [Gross deposit + Cashout Achievement ]/SUM([Deposit Target ])>2 THEN 2 ELSE  [Gross deposit + Cashout Achievement ]/SUM([Deposit Target ]) END
  ```

- **Action Date**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('day', [Date (Custom SQL Query3)])
  ```

- **Active Open Link**

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/AccountManagerTargets_17102292560510/ActiveOpenByCID?:iid=1'
  ```

- **Activities AMs & SAMs By Day Link**

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/Activitiesreports/ActivitiesAMsSAMsByDay?:iid=1'
  ```

- **Activities By Region Link **

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/Activitiesreports/ActivitiesByRegion?:iid=2'
  ```

- **ActivitiesAMsSAMs Link**

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/Activitiesreports/ActivitiesAMsSAMs'
  ```

- **Actual Cashout**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond Cashout] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Cashout] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Cashout+IBAN**

  ```
  [Actual Cashout]+[Actual Close IBAN]
  ```

- **Actual Close IBAN**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond close IBAN] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus close IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalClosetoIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Compensation Contacted **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Contacted],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1 THEN [Diamond Compensation Contacted ] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1 THEN [Platinum Plus Compensation contacted  ] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit'  and [Contacted]=1 THEN [TotalCompensation_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Compensation Not Contacted  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Contacted],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Diamond Compensation Not Contacted ]
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Platinum Plus Compensation Not contacted ]
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit'  and [Contacted]=0 THEN [TotalCompensation_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Contacted Deposit **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query2) #1]  AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Contacted Deposit' THEN  [ActualContactDeposit (Custom SQL Query2)]
    ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Deposit**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond Deposit] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Deposit] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)]  AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Deposit AM**

  ```
  [ActualContactDeposit (Custom SQL Query2)]
  ```

- **Actual Deposit Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Contacted],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1 THEN [Diamond Deposit Contacted] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1 THEN [Platinum Plus Deposit contacted ] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit'  and [Contacted]=1 THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Deposit Not Contacted **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Diamond Deposit] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Platinum Plus Deposit Not contacted] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]:
  (SUM([Actual Deposit+IBAN Contacted])+SUM([Actual Compensation Contacted ])*1.5)*1.2+(SUM([Actual Deposit+IBAN  Not Contacted])+SUM([Actual Compensation Not Contacted  ])*1.5)*0.8}
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]:
  SUM([Actual Deposit+IBAN Contacted])*1.2+SUM([Actual Deposit+IBAN  Not Contacted])*0.8}
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN  (withount *)**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Contacted]:SUM(
  (([Actual Deposit Contacted])+([Actual Open IBAN Contacted]))
  +
  (([Actual Deposit Not Contacted ])+([Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted ])))}
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN  (withount *)**

  ```
  (([Actual Deposit Contacted])+([Actual Open IBAN Contacted]))
  +
  (([Actual Deposit Not Contacted ])+([Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted ]))
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN  Not Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]:sum((([Actual Deposit Not Contacted ])+([Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted ])))}
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN +Compensation Not Contacted (copy)**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]:sum((([Actual Deposit Not Contacted ])+([Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted ])+[Actual Compensation Not Contacted  ]))}
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Contacted]:((SUM([Actual Deposit Contacted])+SUM([Actual Open IBAN Contacted])))}
  ```

- **Actual Deposit+IBAN+Compensation Contacted (copy)**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Contacted]:((SUM([Actual Deposit Contacted])+SUM([Actual Open IBAN Contacted])+ SUM([Actual Compensation Contacted ])))}
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[Contacted]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [Contacted]=1 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1  THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=1 and [Club (Custom SQL Query7)] in ('Platinum Plus', 'Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [Contacted]=0 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=0 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **AM Deposit Achievement in %  **

  ```
  IF SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) >1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE  SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) END
  ```

- **AM Engagement Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Engagement' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Achievement**

  ```
  if [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ])>1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ]) END
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation **

  ```
  SUM([Actual MoneyIn (copy)_1240178748756172801])+IFNULL( SUM([Invested in campaign with contact  (copy)_783626348631248896])*0.2,0)
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn AM' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM Total Achievement**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([QC Achievement %]) THEN 
      IF [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ] > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]
      END
  ELSE 
      IF ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 
      END
  END
  ```

- **AM Total Achievement**

  ```
  IF ([Engagement Achievement in % ]+[AM Deposit Achievement in %  ] + [AM MoneyIn Achievement] )/3>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE ([Engagement Achievement in % ]+[AM Deposit Achievement in %  ] + [AM MoneyIn Achievement] )/3 END
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Achievement in %  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[Date],[region],[Contact Upgrade],[IsUpgrade]:
  IF MIN([Contact Upgrade]) = 1 AND MIN([IsUpgrade]) = 1 THEN
          IF COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) >1.5 THEN 1.5 
  ELSE  COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) END
  END}
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Achievement in %  **

  ```
  IF COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) >1.5 THEN 1.5 ELSE  COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) END
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Upgrade from Platinum' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **Amount dep**

  ```
  { FIXED  [RealCID], [Action Date],[Account Manager],[ActionType (Custom SQL Query3)],[AccountType]:SUM([Amount])}
  ```

- **Amount To Upgrade**

  ```
  50000 - [ClubEquity]
  ```

- **AO Achievement**

  ```
  IF  [AO Actual Ratio]<=max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy 2)**

  ```
  IF  INT([AO Actual Ratio])<=INT(max([AO Portfolio benchmark] )) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  IF  [RM AO old]<max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN 0.25
  ELSEIF [RM AO old]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN

- **AO Portfolio benchmark (copy)**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

  ```

- **Cash out ratio benchmark  cat**

  ```
  if SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) })>0.9 THEN 0.9 ELSE
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) }) END
  ```

             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit')

  ```

  ```

  END}

  END

- **RM AO old**

  ```
  IF  MAX([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF MAX([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **test not  contact dep **

  ```
  if [Contacted (Custom SQL Query3)]=0 then ([Amount])*0.8 end
  ```

- **Total Achievement **

  ```
  IF ([trustpilot ]>=SUM([Trustpilot Target  ])) THEN
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1.25 THEN 1.25 
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  ELSE 
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1 THEN 1
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  end
  ```

- **Total Achievement **

  ```
  IF ([trustpilot ]>=SUM([Trustpilot Target  ])) THEN
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [Total Achievement KPI3] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1.25 THEN 1.25 
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [Total Achievement KPI3] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  ELSE 
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [Total Achievement KPI3] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1 THEN 1
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [Total Achievement KPI3] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  end
  ```

- **Total Achievement KPI3**

  ```
  IFNULL(FLOAT([PI Meeting Achievement]),0)*0.2+IFNULL(FLOAT([MoneyIn Achievement ]),0)*0.8
  ```

- **Total Cashout  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX( [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]) }
  ```

- **Total Cashout   (copy)**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX( [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]) }
  ```

- **Total Close from IBAN**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX([TotalClosetoIBAN_ThisMonth] ) }
  ```

- **Total Deposit **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX( [TotalDeposits_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]) }
  ```

- **Total Engagement**

  ```
  [Completed Mail By Working Day]+[Completed Phone By Working Day]+[Whatsapp By Working Day]
  ```

- **Total Open from IBAN**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX([TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth] ) }
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement**

  ```
  (IF  [RM Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Deposit Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM Trigger Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Trigger Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM MoneyIn Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM MoneyIn Achievement ] END +
  IF  [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM AM QC achievemnt]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM QC achievemnt] END
  ) * 0.1
  +
  (IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSEif [RM Net Deposit Achievement]<0 THEN 0 ELSE [RM Net Deposit Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Revenue Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Revenue Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Club Member Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Club Member Achievement ]END 
  )*40/3/100
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement**

  ```
  (IF  [RM Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Deposit Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM Trigger Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Trigger Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM MoneyIn Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM MoneyIn Achievement ] END +
  IF  [RM AM Contacted Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM Contacted Deposit Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM AM Engagement Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM Engagement Achievement] END + 
  IF  [RM AM MoneyIn Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM MoneyIn Achievement ] END
  ) * 0.1
  +
  (IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSEif [RM Net Deposit Achievement]<0 THEN 0 ELSE [RM Net Deposit Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Revenue Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Revenue Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Club Member Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Club Member Achievement ]END 
  )*40/3/100
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  ([RM Deposit Achievement]+[RM Trigger Achievement]+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]+[RM AM Upgrade Achievement]+[RM AM QC achievemnt]+[RM AM Engagement Achievement])*0.1
  + ([RM Net Deposit Achievement]+[RM Revenue Achievement]+[RM Club Member Achievement ])*40/3/100
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  ([RM Deposit Achievement]+[RM Trigger Achievement]+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]+[RM AM Contacted Deposit Achievement]+[RM AM MoneyIn Achievement ]+[RM AM Engagement Achievement])*0.1
  + ([RM Net Deposit Achievement]+[RM Revenue Achievement]+[RM Club Member Achievement ])*40/3/100
  ```

  ```

  ```

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query2)],[Date Up]
  : max( [WhatsApp (Custom SQL Query2)]) }
  ```

- **Whatsapp By Working Day**

  ```
  SUM(IF  [ActionType] = 'Whatsapp' THEN [NumOfCall] ELSE 0 end)/SUM([Working Day])
  ```

- **Whatsapp per day**

  ```
  SUM([Whatsapp])/SUM([Working Day])
  ```

- **Working Day**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)],  [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID],[Date] : 
  MAX(IF  
  ([NumOfCall]>2 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('CompletedPhone'))
  or ([NumOfCall]>7 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('InboundEmail'))
    THEN 1 ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Yesterday**

  ```
  [Date Up]= DATEADD('day', -1, TODAY())
  ```

### Workbook: Account Manager Targets 2025_TOM

- ** Deposit Calculation**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: 
     MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND 
             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') 
         THEN [Actual Deposit+IBAN ]
     END) 
  }
  ```

  (COUNTD([Id])-COUNTD([Expierd]))/COUNTD([Id])
  ```

  ```

  ```

  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Cashout]

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[Contacted]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [Contacted]=1 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1  THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=1 and [Club (Custom SQL Query7)] in ('Platinum Plus', 'Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [Contacted]=0 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=0 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **AM Deposit Achievement in %  **

  ```
  IF SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) >1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE  SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) END
  ```

- **AM Engagement Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Engagement' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Achievement**

  ```
  if [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ])>1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ]) END
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation **

  ```
  SUM([Actual MoneyIn (copy)_1240178748756172801])+IFNULL( SUM([Invested in campaign with contact  (copy)_783626348631248896])*0.2,0)
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn AM' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM Total Achievement**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([QC Achievement %]) THEN 
      IF [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ] > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]
      END
  ELSE 
      IF ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 
      END
  END
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Achievement in %  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[Date],[region],[Contact Upgrade],[IsUpgrade]:
  IF MIN([Contact Upgrade]) = 1 AND MIN([IsUpgrade]) = 1 THEN
          IF COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) >1.5 THEN 1.5 
  ELSE  COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) END
  END}
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Upgrade from Platinum' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **Amount dep**

  ```
  { FIXED  [RealCID], [Action Date],[Account Manager],[ActionType (Custom SQL Query3)],[AccountType]:SUM([Amount])}
  ```

- **Amount To Upgrade**

  ```
  50000 - [ClubEquity]
  ```

- **AO Achievement**

  ```
  IF  [AO Actual Ratio]<=max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy 2)**

  ```
  IF  INT([AO Actual Ratio])<=INT(max([AO Portfolio benchmark] )) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  IF  [RM AO old]<max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN 0.25
  ELSEIF [RM AO old]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio (copy)**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **AO Diamond **

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }
  ```

  ```

  ```

- **AO Portfolio benchmark (copy)**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

- **AO Ratio AVG 6 Months**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: AVG(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN (([AO Diamond ]/[EOM Diamond])*1 + ([AO Platinum Plus ]/[EOM Platinum Plus])*9)/10 END) }
  ```

- **Cash out ratio benchmark  cat**

  ```
  if SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) })>0.9 THEN 0.9 ELSE
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) }) END
  ```

             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') 
         THEN [Actual Cashout+IBAN] 
     END) 
  }
  ```

  ELSE (sum ( [Actual Cashout+IBAN])/ ([final without *]) ) END
  ```

  ```

- **Revenue * 13.33%**

  ```
  IF [RM Revenue Achievement]*13.33/100>0.1333 THEN 0.1333 else [RM Revenue Achievement]*13.33/100 END
  ```

- **RM AM 30%**

  ```
  IF [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]*0.15+[RM AM QC achievemnt]*0.15>0.3 THEN 0.3
  ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]*0.15+[RM AM QC achievemnt]*0.15 END
  ```

- **RM AM Engagement**

  ```
  { FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date] : ([Engagement Achievement in % ])}
  ```

- **RM AM Engagement Achievement**

  ```
  AVG([RM AM Engagement])
  ```

- **RM AM MoneyIn**

  ```
  { FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date] : ([AM MoneyIn Achievement])}
  ```

- **RM AM QC achievemnt**

  ```
  if AVG([RM QC])>1 then 1 else AVG([RM QC]) end
  ```

- **RM AM Upgrade**

  ```
  { FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date] :SUM ([AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ])}
  ```

- **RM AM Upgrade Achievement**

  ```
  IF AVG([RM AM Upgrade])>1 then 1 else  AVG([RM AM Upgrade]) end
  ```

- **RM AO old**

  ```
  IF  MAX([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF MAX([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **RM Club member Achievement **

  ```
  IF (MAX([ClubMember]))/(MAX([RM Club Member Target]))>1 THEN 1 ELSE (MAX([ClubMember]))/(MAX([RM Club Member Target])) END
  ```

- **RM Club Member Achievement **

  ```
  IF  MAX([ClubMember])>=SUM([RM Club Member Target]) THEN MAX([ClubMember])/SUM([RM Club Member Target]) 
  ELSEIF (MAX([ClubMember])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))/(SUM([RM Club Member Target])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))>1 THEN 1 ELSE (MAX([ClubMember])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))/(SUM([RM Club Member Target])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ])) END
  ```

  { FIXED[region],[type_of_kpi],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date] :MAX(IF  [type_of_kpi] = 'Club Members' THEN [target] ELSE NULL end)}
  ```

  ```

  ```

- **SAM *30%**

  ```
  IF ([RM Deposit Achievement]*0.1+[RM Trigger Achievement]*0.1+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]*0.1)>0.3 THEN 0.3
  ELSE ([RM Deposit Achievement]*0.1+[RM Trigger Achievement]*0.1+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]*0.1) END
  ```

- **SAM *30% (copy)**

  ```
  { INCLUDE [Account Manager] :
  
  if MAX([Position_Filter_Num]) = 1 
  then
  (
  IF ([RM Deposit Achievement]*0.1+[RM Trigger Achievement]*0.1+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]*0.1)>0.3 THEN 0.3
  ELSE ([RM Deposit Achievement]*0.1+[RM Trigger Achievement]*0.1+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]*0.1) END
  
  )
  END
  }
  ```

- **Solved**

  IF [Status__c]='5' then [Id] end
  ```

  ```

- **Total Achievement **

  ```
  IF ([trustpilot ]>=SUM([Trustpilot Target  ])) THEN
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1.25 THEN 1.25 
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  ELSE 
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1 THEN 1
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  end
  ```

  ```

- **Total RM Achievement**

  ```
  (IF  [RM Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Deposit Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM Trigger Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Trigger Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM MoneyIn Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM MoneyIn Achievement ] END +
  IF  [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM AM QC achievemnt]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM QC achievemnt] END
  ) * 0.1
  +
  (IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSEif [RM Net Deposit Achievement]<0 THEN 0 ELSE [RM Net Deposit Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Revenue Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Revenue Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Club Member Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Club Member Achievement ]END 
  )*40/3/100
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  ([RM Deposit Achievement]+[RM Trigger Achievement]+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]+[RM AM Upgrade Achievement]+[RM AM QC achievemnt]+[RM AM Engagement Achievement])*0.1
  + ([RM Net Deposit Achievement]+[RM Revenue Achievement]+[RM Club Member Achievement ])*40/3/100
  ```

  ```

- **Working Day**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)],  [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID],[Date] : 
  MAX(IF  
  ([NumOfCall]>2 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('CompletedPhone'))
  or ([NumOfCall]>7 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('InboundEmail'))
    THEN 1 ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

  ```

     END) 
  }

  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[Contacted]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [Contacted]=1 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1  THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=1 and [Club (Custom SQL Query7)] in ('Platinum Plus', 'Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=0 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }

- **AM Deposit Achievement in %  **

  ```
  IF SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) >1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE  SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) END
  ```

- **AM Engagement Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Engagement' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Achievement**

  ```
  if [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ])>1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ]) END
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation **

  ```
  SUM([Actual MoneyIn (copy)_1240178748756172801])+IFNULL( SUM([Invested in campaign with contact  (copy)_783626348631248896])*0.2,0)
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn AM' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM Total Achievement**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([QC Achievement %]) THEN 
      IF [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ] > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]
      END
  ELSE 
      IF ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 
      END
  END
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Achievement in %  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[Date],[region],[Contact Upgrade],[IsUpgrade]:
  IF MIN([Contact Upgrade]) = 1 AND MIN([IsUpgrade]) = 1 THEN
          IF COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) >1.5 THEN 1.5 
  ELSE  COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) END
  END}
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Upgrade from Platinum' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **Amount dep**

  ```
  { FIXED  [RealCID], [Action Date],[Account Manager],[ActionType (Custom SQL Query3)],[AccountType]:SUM([Amount])}
  ```

- **Amount To Upgrade**

  ```
  50000 - [ClubEquity]
  ```

- **AO Achievement**

  ```
  IF  [AO Actual Ratio]<=max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy 2)**

  ```
  IF  INT([AO Actual Ratio])<=INT(max([AO Portfolio benchmark] )) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  IF  [RM AO old]<max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN 0.25
  ELSEIF [RM AO old]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio (copy)**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **AO Diamond **

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }

  ```

- **AO Portfolio benchmark (copy)**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

- **AO Ratio AVG 6 Months**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: AVG(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate] THEN (([AO Diamond ]/[EOM Diamond])*1 + ([AO Platinum Plus ]/[EOM Platinum Plus])*9)/10 END) }

- **Cash out ratio benchmark  cat**

  ```
  if SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) })>0.9 THEN 0.9 ELSE
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) }) END
  ```

     MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND 
             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') 
         THEN [Actual Cashout+IBAN] 
     END) 
  }
  ```

- **Cashout ratio Achievement **

  ```
  IF (sum ( [Actual Cashout+IBAN])/ ([final without *]) )>1 THEN 1 
  
  ELSE (sum ( [Actual Cashout+IBAN])/ ([final without *]) ) END
  ```

  ```
  IF (sum ( [Actual Cashout+IBAN])/sum ([Actual Deposit+IBAN  (withount *)]) )>1 THEN 1 
  
  ELSE (sum ( [Actual Cashout+IBAN])/sum ([Actual Deposit+IBAN  (withount *)]) ) END
  ```

  ```

- **MoneyIn Contacted  *1**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[Contacted (Custom SQL Query6)],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query6)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query6)] and [Contacted (Custom SQL Query6)]=1 and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [Diamond MoneyIn] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query6)] and [Contacted (Custom SQL Query6)]=1 and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [Platinum Plus MoneyIn Contacted] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query6)] AND [Contacted (Custom SQL Query6)]=1 and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [MoneyIn (Custom SQL Query6)]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **MoneyIn final amount for calculation **

  ```

  //update by Adi for 2026: not contacted=0.5, cotacted=1, produxt of the month=0.5
  ```

  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query6)] and [Contacted (Custom SQL Query6)]=0 and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [Platinum Plus MoneyIn Contacted]

- **New Region**

  ```
  IF  [region] IN ('UK - Platinum Plus','UK - Diamond','Vyacheslav Zagalski','Harry Charitou') THEN 'UK' ELSE [region] END
  ```

- **Nt Deposit *13.33%**

  ```
  IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]*13.33/100>0.1333 then 0.1333 else [RM Net Deposit Achievement]*13.33/100 END
  ```

- **Number Of Attempted Phone**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)], [ActionType], [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID] : 
  MAX(IF [ActionType] = 'Contacted__c' THEN [NumberOfCall (Custom SQL Query2)] ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Number Of Completed Mail**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)], [ActionType], [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID] : 
  MAX(IF [ActionType] = 'Completed_Contact_Email__c'  THEN [NumberOfCall (Custom SQL Query2)] ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Number Of Completed Phone**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)], [ActionType] : 
  MAX(IF [ActionType] = 'Phone_Call_Succeed__c' THEN [NumberOfCall (Custom SQL Query2)] ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **PI Meeting Achievement**

  ```
  IF  MAX([PI Meeting Final])/MAX([PI Meeting Target ])>1 THEN 1 ELSE MAX([PI Meeting Final])/MAX([PI Meeting Target ]) end
  ```

- **PI Meeting Final**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi (Custom SQL Query6)],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi (Custom SQL Query6)] = 'PI Meeting' THEN [achievment] END)}
  ```

- **PI Meeting Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi (Custom SQL Query6)],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi (Custom SQL Query6)] = 'PI Meeting' THEN [target (Custom SQL Query6)] END)}
  ```

  ```

  ```

  ```

  ```

- **QC Achievement %**

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[Date],[region]:
  IF [AVG QC]>= 90 AND [AVG QC] <= 100 THEN 1
      ELSEIF  [AVG QC] >= 80 AND [AVG QC] <= 89 THEN 0.75
      ELSEIF [AVG QC] >= 70 AND [AVG QC] <= 79 THEN 0.5
      ELSEIF [AVG QC] >= 1 AND [AVG QC] <= 69 THEN 0
  
  END}
  ```

  ```

  ```

  ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]*0.15+[RM AM QC achievemnt]*0.15 END
  ```

- **RM AO old**

  ```
  IF  MAX([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF MAX([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **RM Club Member Achievement **

  ```
  IF  MAX([ClubMember])>=SUM([RM Club Member Target]) THEN MAX([ClubMember])/SUM([RM Club Member Target]) 
  ELSEIF (MAX([ClubMember])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))/(SUM([RM Club Member Target])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))>1 THEN 1 ELSE (MAX([ClubMember])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))/(SUM([RM Club Member Target])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ])) END
  ```

  then

  )
  END
  }

- **Total Achievement **

  ```
  //IF ([trustpilot ]>=SUM([Trustpilot Target  ])) THEN
     // IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1.25 THEN 1.25 
      //ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  //ELSE 
   //   IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1 THEN 1
     // ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  //end
  IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1 and ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 <1.25 THEN 1
  elseif ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >=1.25 THEN 1.25
  else  ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 end
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement**

  ```
  (IF  [RM Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Deposit Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM Trigger Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Trigger Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM MoneyIn Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM MoneyIn Achievement ] END +
  IF  [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM AM QC achievemnt]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM QC achievemnt] END
  ) * 0.1
  +
  (IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSEif [RM Net Deposit Achievement]<0 THEN 0 ELSE [RM Net Deposit Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Revenue Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Revenue Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Club Member Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Club Member Achievement ]END 
  )*40/3/100
  ```
