  ```
  ([RM Deposit Achievement]+[RM Trigger Achievement]+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]+[RM AM Upgrade Achievement]+[RM AM QC achievemnt]+[RM AM Engagement Achievement])*0.1
  + ([RM Net Deposit Achievement]+[RM Revenue Achievement]+[RM Club Member Achievement ])*40/3/100
  ```

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)],  [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID],[Date] : 
  MAX(IF  
  ([NumOfCall]>2 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('CompletedPhone'))
  or ([NumOfCall]>7 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('InboundEmail'))
    THEN 1 ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

### Workbook: Analysis OptIn

#### Datasource: BI_DB_CID_DailyPanel_Club (BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData) 

- **OptInDateGroup**

  ```
  IF YEAR([OptInMonth]) <2023 THEN '<2023'
      ELSE STR(YEAR([OptInMonth]))+'-'+STR(MONTH([OptInMonth])) END
  ```

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (sql_dp_prod_we)

- **Users**

  ```
  COUNT([CID])
  ```

#### Datasource: Opt-In Analysis

- **Avg Balance**

  ```
  SUM([EOM_Balance])/[Users]
  ```

- **Avg Deposit**

  ```
  SUM([TotalDeposits]) /[Users]
  ```

- **Avg NetDeposit**

  ```
  SUM([NetDeposits])/[Users]
  ```

- **CashoutFromEquity**

  ```
  SUM([EquityLastMonth])/SUM([TotalCashouts])
  ```

- **OptInDateGroup**

  ```
  IF YEAR([PlatinumPlusSeniority2023]) <2023 THEN STR(YEAR([PlatinumPlusSeniority2023])) 
      ELSE STR(YEAR([PlatinumPlusSeniority2023]))+'-'+STR(MONTH( [PlatinumPlusSeniority2023])) END
  ```

- **OptInDateGroup1**

  ```
  IF YEAR([OptInDate]) <2023 THEN '<2023'
      ELSE STR(YEAR([OptInDate]))+'-'+STR(MONTH( [OptInDate])) END
  ```

- **SeniorityOptInGroup**

  ```
  IF [SeniorityOptIn] >=24 THEN '+24s Month'
      ELSEIF [SeniorityOptIn] >=12 THEN '12-24 Months'
          ELSEIF [SeniorityOptIn] >=6 THEN '6-12 Months'
              ELSEIF [SeniorityOptIn] >=3 THEN '3-6 Months'
                  ELSEIF [SeniorityOptIn] >=1 THEN '1-3 Months'
                      ELSEIF [SeniorityOptIn] >=0 THEN '1 Month'
                          ELSE 'NotOptedInYet' END
  ```

- **Users**

  ```
  COUNT([CID])
  ```

### Workbook: IR Dashboard

#### Datasource: AUA

- **AUA O.B**

  ```
  LOOKUP(SUM([Amount]), -1)
  ```

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Date Filter For Cycle**

  ```
  RANK_UNIQUE(MAX([Date]), 'desc') <= [Months to Display]
  ```

- **info**

  ```
  max(1)
  ```

- **LoadDate AUA**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

- **PnL**

  ```
  SUM([Amount]) 
  - LOOKUP(SUM([Amount]), -1)
  - SUM([federated.1ifznqu042lok517q8dp405bhxhu].[Deposits])
  + SUM([federated.1ifznqu042lok517q8dp405bhxhu].[Calculation_1800313983448879119])
  ```

#### Datasource: Avg Staking

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **info**

  ```
  max(1)
  ```

- **Staking LoadDate**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

#### Datasource: Client funds

- **Avg Cash**

  ```
  sum([Total Cash])/max([Num_of_days])
  ```

- **Avg CFD (w/o FSA & FSRA)**

  ```
  sum([CFD Equity])/max([Num_of_days])
  ```

- **CFD Equity**

  ```
  if [Regulation] in ('FSA Seychelles','FSRA') THEN 0 ELSE  [Equity CFD] end
  ```

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Load Date Client funds**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 
  or dATEDIFF('day', MAX(([federated.0noh3780xdqner15ynnod11h8snh].[LoadDate])), TODAY()) > 0
  or dATEDIFF('day', MAX(([federated.1behsvt1wcebwa172y52s1snnzf7].[LoadDate])), TODAY()) > 0
  
  
  
  THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

- **Total Interest Client Balance**

  ```
  ZN([Avg CFD (w/o FSA & FSRA)])+ZN([Avg Cash])+SUM(ZN([federated.1behsvt1wcebwa172y52s1snnzf7].[AvgOpenPosition]))+SUM(ZN([federated.1hw9a300zmwbgk1bxwbtg1qngkdv].[Avg_eMoney_BalanceUSD]))+SUM(ZN([federated.0noh3780xdqner15ynnod11h8snh].[Avg_Value_OptIn]))
  ```

#### Datasource: Club

- **Funded/ Depositors**

  ```
  IF [IsEOM_Funded_NEW] = 1 THEN "Funded EOQ"
  ELSE "Depositors"
  END
  ```

- **Type**

  ```
  IF [UserType] = "Club" OR [UserType] = "Non-Club" THEN "All"
  ELSE "Other"
  END
  ```

- **view filter**

  ```
  IF [Users Filter] = "Depositors" THEN
      [IsEOM_Funded_NEW] = 0 OR [IsEOM_Funded_NEW] = 1    
  ELSE // "Funded EOQ"
      [IsEOM_Funded_NEW] = 1                      
  END
  ```

#### Datasource: Commission By Asset 

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Load Data Commission**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

#### Datasource: Copy

- **info**

  ```
  max(1)
  ```

#### Datasource: Deposits + Withdrawals

- **CashoutsAdjusted_Negative**

  ```
  [CashoutsAdjusted]*-1
  ```

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **LoadDate Money transfers**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 
  or dATEDIFF('day', MAX(([federated.0nou0gd1syfahr19g5pys03c73c9].[LoadDate])), TODAY()) > 0
  
  
  
  
  THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

- **Total Money Transfer**

  ```
  sum(ZN([CashoutsAdjusted]))+SUM(ZN([Deposits]))+sum(ZN([federated.0nou0gd1syfahr19g5pys03c73c9].[Trade_from_IBAN_Amount]))
  ```

#### Datasource: eMoney_Balance

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

#### Datasource: Funded

- **Churn**

  ```
  SUM([Funded_EOM]) 
  - (LOOKUP(SUM([Funded_EOM]), -1)
  + sum([New_Funded]))
  ```

- **Date Filter**

  ```
  DATEDIFF('month', [Date], TODAY()) < [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Date Filter for cycle**

  ```
  RANK_UNIQUE(MAX([Date]), 'desc') <= [Months to Display]
  ```

- **Funded Accounts O.B**

  ```
  LOOKUP(SUM([Funded_EOM]), -1)
  ```

- **Load date funded**

  ```
  IF DATEDIFF('day', MAX([LoadDate]), TODAY()) > 0 THEN "⚠️ Not updated today" ELSE "✅ Last Updated: " + STR(MAX([LoadDate])) END
  ```

### Workbook: MIMO Dashboard - New 27.12.23

#### Datasource: By FundingType

- **%Change Last 5 Months Avg. **

  ```
  [Last 5 Months Avg.KPI]/[Previous Month KPI]-1
  ```

- **%Change Previous Month**

  ```
  [Last Month KPI ]/[Previous Month KPI]-1
  ```

- **Approved (copy)**

  ```
  [Approved]
  ```

- **Choose KPI 4**

  ```
  sum(if [Choose KPI4]='Total Amount' then [AmountUSD] else [Transactions] end)
  ```

- **IsLast5Months**

  ```
  [Month]<DATEADD('month',-2,TODAY())
  and [Month]>DATEADD('month',-7,TODAY())
  ```

- **IsLastMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[Month],today())=1 then TRUE END
  ```

- **IsPreviousMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[Month],today())=2 then TRUE END
  ```

- **IsThisMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[Month],today())=0 then TRUE else FALSE END
  ```

- **Last 5 Months Avg.KPI**

  ```
  [Choose KPI 4]/5
  ```

- **Last Month KPI **

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth]=TRUE and [Choose KPI4]='Total Amount' then [AmountUSD] else [Transactions] END)
  ```

- **Previous Month KPI**

  ```
  sum(if [IsPreviousMonth]=TRUE and [Choose KPI4]='Total Amount' then [AmountUSD] else [Transactions] END)
  ```

- **Amount Pareto**

  ```
  sum(if [Choose Pareto KPI]='Total Deposits' then [TotalDeposits] else [TotalCashouts] end)
  ```

- **Avg. Cashout  Format 2  **

  ```

  ```

- **Avg. Deposits LAst 5 Month**

  ```
  AVG([Avg.Deposit Monthly])
  ```

- **Avg.Cashout Format 3  **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Avg.Cashout',[Choose KPI 3],NULL)
  ```

- **Avg.Cashout Format 3  5 Months Avg.**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Avg.Cashout',[Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.],NULL)
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts**

  ```
  sum([TotalCashouts])/COUNTD(if [TotalCashouts]>0 then [CID] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts LAst 5 Month **

  ```
  AVG([Avg.Cashouts Monthly])
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts Monthly**

  ```
  { FIXED [ActiveDate]:sum([TotalCashouts])/COUNTD(if [TotalCashouts]>0 then [CID] else null end)}
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts Previois Month**

  ```
  [Total Cashouts Previous Month]/[Unique Cashouts Previous Month]
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts This Month**

  ```
  [Total Cashouts This Month]/[Unique Cashouts  This Month]
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit**

  ```
  sum([TotalDeposits])/COUNTD(if [TotalDeposits]>0 then [CID] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit Format 2  **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI2]='Avg.Deposit',[Choose KPI 2],NULL)
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit Format 3**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Avg.Deposit',[Choose KPI 3],NULL)
  ```

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Avg.Deposit',[Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.],NULL)
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit Monthly**

  ```
  { FIXED [ActiveDate]:sum([TotalDeposits])/COUNTD(if [TotalDeposits]>0 then [CID] else null end)}
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit Previous Month**

  ```
  [Total Deposits PrevMonth]/[Unique Depositors  Previous Month]
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit This Month**

  ```
  [Total Deposits This Month]/[Unique Depositors This Month]
  ```

- **Choose KPI 1**

  ```
  IF [Choose KPI1]='Total Deposits' then sum([TotalDeposits])
  ELSEIF  [Choose KPI1]='Total Cashouts' then sum([TotalCashouts])
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI1]='Unique Depositors' then [Unique Depositors ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI1]='Unique Cashouts' then [Unique Cashouts ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI1]='Net Deposits' then[Net Deposits]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI1]='Avg.Deposit' then[Avg.Deposit]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI1]='Avg.Cashout' then[Avg.Cashouts]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI1]='CO/Deposit Ratio' then [CO/Deposit Ratio] 
  END
  ```

- **Choose KPI 2**

  ```
  IF [Choose KPI2]='Total Deposits' then sum([TotalDeposits])
  ELSEIF  [Choose KPI2]='Total Cashouts' then sum([TotalCashouts])
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI2]='Unique Depositors' then [Unique Depositors ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI2]='Unique Cashouts' then [Unique Cashouts ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI2]='Net Deposits' then[Net Deposits]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI2]='Avg.Deposit' then[Avg.Deposit]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI2]='Avg.Cashout' then[Avg.Cashouts]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI2]='CO/Deposit Ratio' then [CO/Deposit Ratio] 
  END
  ```

- **Choose KPI 3**

  ```
  IF [Choose KPI3]='Total Deposits' then sum([TotalDeposits])
  ELSEIF  [Choose KPI3]='Total Cashouts' then sum([TotalCashouts])
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Unique Depositors' then [Unique Depositors ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Unique Cashouts' then [Unique Cashouts ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Net Deposits' then[Net Deposits]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Avg.Deposit' then[Avg.Deposit]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Avg.Cashout' then[Avg.Cashouts]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='CO/Deposit Ratio' then [CO/Deposit Ratio] 
  END
  ```

- **Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.**

  ```
  IF [Choose KPI3]='Total Deposits' then [Total Deposits Avg. 5 Months]
  ELSEIF  [Choose KPI3]='Total Cashouts' then [Total Cashouts Avg. 5 Months ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Unique Depositors' then [Unique Depositors Avg 5 Month]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Unique Cashouts' then [Unique Cashouts Avg 5 Month ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Net Deposits' then [Net Deposits Avg.5 Months]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Avg.Deposit' then [Avg. Deposits LAst 5 Month]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='Avg.Cashout' then [Avg.Cashouts LAst 5 Month ]
  ELSEIF [Choose KPI3]='CO/Deposit Ratio' then [CO/Dep Avg 5 Months]
  END
  ```

- **Choose Pareto KPI**

  ```
  [Choose Pareto KPI]
  ```

- **CID Pareto**

  ```
  if [Choose Pareto KPI]='Total Deposits' then [Unique Depositors ] else [Unique Cashouts ] end
  ```

- **CO/Dep Avg 5 Months**

  ```
  [Total Cashouts Avg. 5 Months ]/[Total Deposits Avg. 5 Months]
  ```

- **CO/Deposit Ratio**

  ```
  sum([TotalCashouts])/sum([TotalDeposits])
  ```

- **CO/Deposit Ratio Format 2**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI2]='CO/Deposit Ratio',[Choose KPI 2],NULL)
  ```

- **CO/Deposit Ratio Format 3 **

  ```

  ```

  ```

  [Total Cashouts Previous Month]/[Total Deposits PrevMonth]
  ```

- **CO/Deposit Ratio This Month**

  ```
  [Total Cashouts This Month]/[Total Deposits This Month]
  ```

- **Deposit Group**

  ```
  IF [CountDeposits]=1 and [IsFTD_ThisM]=0 then 'one time depositor'
  ELSEIF [CountDeposits]=1 and [IsFTD_ThisM]=1 then 'FTD Only'
  else 'more than one time depositor' end
  ```

- **IsActive**

  ```
  if [TotalDeposits]>0 or [TotalCashouts]>0 then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **IsDepositor**

  ```
  if [CountDeposits]>0 then 1 else 0 end
  ```

- **IsLast Month**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[ActiveDate],today())=1 then TRUE END
  ```

- **IsLast5M**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]<DATEADD('month',-2,TODAY())
  and [ActiveDate]>DATEADD('month',-7,TODAY())
  ```

- **IsPreviousMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[ActiveDate],today())=2 then TRUE END
  ```

- **IsThisMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[ActiveDate],today())=0 then TRUE else FALSE END
  ```

- **MIMO_Segment**

  ```
  if [TotalDeposits]>0 and [TotalCashouts]=0 then 'Only Deposit'
  ELSEIF [TotalDeposits]=0 and [TotalCashouts]>0 then 'Only Cashout'
  ELSEIF [TotalDeposits]>0 and [TotalCashouts]>0 then 'Both Deposit & Cashout'
  else 'No MIMO Activity' end
  ```

- **Net Deposits**

  ```
  SUM([TotalDeposits])-sum([TotalCashouts])
  ```

- **Net Deposits Avg.5 Months**

  ```
  [Total Deposits Avg. 5 Months]-[Total Cashouts Avg. 5 Months ]
  ```

- **Net Deposits Format 2 **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI2]='Net Deposits',[Choose KPI 2],NULL)
  ```

- **Net Deposits Format 3**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Net Deposits',[Choose KPI 3],NULL)
  ```

- **Net Deposits Format 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Net Deposits',[Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.],NULL)
  ```

- **Net Deposits Previous Month**

  ```
  [Total Deposits PrevMonth]-[Total Cashouts Previous Month]
  ```

- **Net Deposits This Month**

  ```
  [Total Deposits This Month]-[Total Cashouts This Month]
  ```

- **Percentile**

  ```
  if [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='Total Deposits' and ATTR([Calculation_1026820751583182932])=1 then RANK_PERCENTILE(sum([TotalDeposits]))
  ELSEIF [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='Total Cashouts' then RANK_PERCENTILE(sum([TotalCashouts]))
  ELSEIF [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='Net Deposits' then RANK_PERCENTILE([Calculation_1026820749149212682])
  ELSEIF [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='CO/Deposit Ratio' then RANK_PERCENTILE([Calculation_1026820749148196871])
  ELSEIF [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='Unique Depositors' and ATTR([Calculation_1026820751583182932])=1 then RANK_PERCENTILE(sum([CountDeposits]))
  ELSEIF [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='Unique Cashouts' then RANK_PERCENTILE([Unique Cashouts Monthly (copy)_1026820749773918230])/*?*/
  ELSEIF [Parameters].[Parameter 2]='Avg.Deposit' and ATTR([Calculation_1026820751583182932])=1 then RANK_PERCENTILE(sum([TotalCashouts])/sum([CountDeposits]))
  
  
  end
  ```

- **Region_Calc**

  ```
  if [Region] in ('UK','German','Arabic GCC','French','Eastern Europ','North Europ'
  ,'South & Central America','Italian','Other Asia','Australia','Spain') then [Region] else 'Other' end
  ```

- **Selected Method**

  ```
  [Select Calculation Method]
  ```

- **Selected Method cross**

  ```
  [Select Calculation Method]
  ```

- **Seniority Groups**

  ```
  IF 
   [Seniority] >=0  and [Seniority] <= 6 THEN "0-6"
  ELSEIF [Seniority] > 6 and [Seniority] <= 12 THEN "7-12"
  ELSEIF [Seniority] > 12 and [Seniority]<=18   THEN "12-18"
  ELSEIF [Seniority] > 18 and [Seniority]<=24   THEN "18-24"
  ELSEIF [Seniority] > 24 and [Seniority]<=36   THEN "24-36"
  ELSEIF [Seniority] > 36   THEN "36+"
  ELSE "Not Funded" END
  ```

- **Split By**

  ```
  if [Split By]='Club' then [EOM_Club]
  ELSEIF  [Split By]='Regulation' then [EOM_Regulation]
  ELSEIF  [Split By]='Region' then [Region_Calc]
  ELSEIF  [Split By]='Seniority' then [Seniority Groups]
  ELSEIF  [Split By]='Cluster' then [ClusterDetail]
  ELSEIF [Split By]='Deposit Group' then [Deposit Group]
  else ''
  END
  ```

- **Split By 2**

  ```
  if [Split By 2]='Club' then [EOM_Club]
  ELSEIF  [Split By 2]='Regulation' then [EOM_Regulation]
  ELSEIF  [Split By 2]='Region' then [Region_Calc]
  ELSEIF  [Split By 2]='Seniority' then [Seniority Groups]
  ELSEIF  [Split By 2]='Cluster' then [ClusterDetail]
  ELSEIF [Split By 2]='Deposit Group' then [Deposit Group]
  END
  ```

- **Split By Pareto**

  if [Split By Pareto]='Club' then [EOM_Club]
  ELSEIF  [Split By Pareto]='Regulation' then [EOM_Regulation]
  ELSEIF  [Split By Pareto]='Region' then [Region_Calc]

  END

  ELSEIF  [Split By_CompareBySplit]='Regulation' then [EOM_Regulation]
  ELSEIF  [Split By_CompareBySplit]='Region' then [Region_Calc]

  ELSEIF  [Split By_Cross]='Regulation' then [EOM_Regulation]
  ELSEIF  [Split By_Cross]='Region' then [Region_Calc]
  ELSEIF  [Split By_Cross]='Seniority' then [Seniority Groups]

  ELSEIF [Split By_Cross]='Deposit Group' then [Deposit Group]
  END

- **Total Cashouts Previous Month**

  ```

- **Total Cashouts This Month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast Month]=TRUE then [TotalCashouts] else null end)
  ```

- **Total CO/Deposit Ratio Format**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI1]='CO/Deposit Ratio',[Choose KPI 1],NULL)
  ```

- **Total deposit Format**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI1]='Total Deposits',[Choose KPI 1],NULL)
  ```

- **Total Deposits Avg. 5 Months**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast5M] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)/5
  ```

- **Total Deposits Format 2**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI2]='Total Deposits',[Choose KPI 2],NULL)
  ```

- **Total Deposits Format 3**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Total Deposits',[Choose KPI 3],NULL)
  ```

- **Total Deposits Format 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Total Deposits',[Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.],NULL)
  ```

- **Total Deposits PrevMonth**

  ```
  sum(if [IsPreviousMonth]=TRUE then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **Total Deposits This Month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast Month]=TRUE then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **Total Net Deposits Format**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI1]='Net Deposits',[Choose KPI 1],NULL)
  ```

- **Total Unique Cashouts Format **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI1]='Unique Cashouts',[Choose KPI 1],NULL)
  ```

- **Total Unique Depositors Format**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI1]='Unique Depositors',[Choose KPI 1],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Cashout Format 2 **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI2]='Unique Cashout',[Choose KPI 2],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts **

  ```
  COUNTD(if [TotalCashouts]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts  This Month**

  ```
  COUNTD(if [IsLast Month]=TRUE and [TotalCashouts]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts Avg 5 Month **

  ```
  sum([Unique Cashouts Monthly])/COUNTD([ActiveDate])
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts Format 3  **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Unique Cashouts',[Choose KPI 3],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts Format 3  Prev 5 Months Avg.**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Unique Cashouts',[Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts Monthly**

  ```
  { FIXED [ActiveDate]:COUNTD(if [TotalCashouts]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)}
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts Previous Month**

  ```
  COUNTD(if [IsPreviousMonth]=TRUE and [TotalCashouts]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)
  ```

- **Unique Depositors **

  ```
  COUNTD(if [TotalDeposits]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)
  ```

- **Unique Depositors  Previous Month**

  ```
  COUNTD(if [IsPreviousMonth]=TRUE and [TotalDeposits]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)
  ```

- **Unique Depositors Avg 5 Month**

  ```
  sum([Unique Depositors Monthly])/COUNTD([ActiveDate])
  ```

- **Unique Depositors Format 2 **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI2]='Unique Depositors',[Choose KPI 2],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Depositors Format 3  **

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Unique Depositors ',[Choose KPI 3],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Depositors Format 3  Prev 5 Months Avg.**

  ```
  IIF([Choose KPI3]='Unique Depositors ',[Choose KPI 3 Prev 5 Months Avg.],NULL)
  ```

- **Unique Depositors Monthly**

  ```
  { FIXED [ActiveDate]: COUNTD(if [TotalDeposits]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)}
  ```

- **Unique Depositors This Month**

  ```
  COUNTD(if [IsLast Month]=TRUE and [TotalDeposits]>0 then [CID] else NULL end)
  ```

### Workbook: Monthly Club Overview

#### Datasource: BI_DB_CID_DailyPanel_Club (BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_DailyPanel_Club)+ (sql_dp_prod_we)

- **ActiveDate**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date])
  ```

- **CalendarQ**

  ```
  REPLACE([Calendar Year Qtr],'-','Q')
  ```

- **Club Members**

  ```
  COUNTD([CID])
  ```

- **Club Region**

  ```
  IF [Name (Dim Country)] IN ('Denmark','Finland','Netherlands','Norway','Sweden') THEN 'Nordic'
  ELSEIF  [Name (Dim Country)] IN ('Poland','Romania','Slovakia','Slovenia','Czech Republic') THEN 'EE'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('South & Central America','Spain') THEN 'Spanish'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('Other Asia','China') THEN 'SEA'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('Arabic Other','Arabic GCC') THEN 'Arabic'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('French','German','Italian','UK','USA','Australia') THEN [Region]
  ELSE 'ROW' END
  ```

- **Cub Tier - First From**

  ```
  { FIXED [CID]: MIN([Sort (Dim PlayerLevel)])}
  ```

- **Cub Tier - Last Upgrade**

  ```
  { FIXED [CID]: MAX([Sort])}
  ```

- **HighLow Target**

  ```
  MAX([LowHighTierTarget])
  ```

- **Is FirstTime Club**

  ```
  [Is FTC]
  ```

- **IsUpgrade**

  ```
  [Is Upgrade]
  ```

- **RegionFilter**

  ```
  IF [Marketing Region Manual Name] = [Region] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Region] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **RegulationFilter **

  ```
  IF [Regulation] = [Regulation] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Regulation] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **Reporting Month**

  ```
  [ActiveDate] = [Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe long**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Long]+1,[Reporting Month])
  and [ActiveDate]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe Short**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Short],[Reporting Month])
  and [ActiveDate]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

#### Datasource: BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData (BI_DB_dbo.BI_DB_CID_MonthlyPanel_FullData) (sql_dp_prod_we)

- **# Products**

  ```
  [Total_Products]
  ```

- **# Products Last**

  ```
  [Total_Products_Last]
  ```

- **% Club AO from Club**

  ```
  SUM([Active Users - report])/[Users]
  ```

- **% Club AO from Total**

  ```
  SUM([Active Users - report])/SUM({ FIXED : SUM([Active Users - report])})
  ```

- **% Club Cash Out from Total**

  ```
  [Club Cash Out]/SUM({ FIXED DATETRUNC('month', [Active Date]): [Total Cash Out]})
  ```

- **% Club Deposit from Total**

  ```
  [Club Deposit]/SUM({ FIXED DATETRUNC('month', [Active Date]): [Total Deposit]})
  ```

- **% Club Revenue from Total**

  ```
  [Club Revenue]/SUM({ FIXED DATETRUNC('month', [Active Date]): [Total Revenue]})
  ```

- **Active **

  ```
  [Active Users - report]
  ```

- **Active Users - report**

  ```
  //SUM(IF [Active Definiton] = 1 THEN [Active Open] ELSE [Active] END)
  IF [Active Definiton] = 1 THEN [Active Open] 
  ELSEIF [Active Definiton] = 2 THEN [Active] 
  ELSEIF [Active Definiton] = 3 THEN [ActiveOpenManual] 
  ELSEIF [Active Definiton] = 4 THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual] END
  ```

- **ARPU**

  ```
  SUM([Revenue Total])/SUM([Active Users - report])
  ```

- **ARPU (High/Low)**

  ```
  { EXCLUDE [EOM Club (group)]: SUM([Revenue Total])/SUM([Active Users - report])}
  ```

- **ARPU Previous Reporting Month**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Previous Reporting Month] THEN [Revenue Total] END)/SUM(IF [Previous Reporting Month] THEN  [Active Users - report] END )
  ```

- **ARPU Reporting Month**

  ```
  SUM(IF [Reporting Month] THEN [Revenue Total] END)/SUM(IF [Reporting Month] THEN  [Active Users - report] END )
  ```

- **Cashout From Deposit**

  ```
  [Total Cash Out]/[Total Deposit]
  ```

- **Change in ARPU**

  ```
  (ZN([ARPU]) - LOOKUP(ZN([ARPU]), -1)) / ABS(LOOKUP(ZN([ARPU]), -1))
  ```

- **Change in ARPU Last Month**

  ```
  MAX({ FIXED [EOM Club (group)]  :([ARPU Reporting Month]/[ARPU Previous Reporting Month])-1})
  ```

- **Change in ARPU Last Month - Shape**

  ```
  IF [Change in ARPU Last Month]>0 THEN 1 
      ELSEIF  [Change in ARPU Last Month]<0 THEN -1
          ELSE 0 END
  ```

- **Club Cash Out**

  ```
  SUM(IF  [EOM Club (group)]!= 'Bronze' THEN [Total Cashouts] END)
  ```

- **Club Deposit**

  ```
  SUM(IF  [EOM Club (group)]!= 'Bronze' THEN [Total Deposits] END)
  ```

- **Club Revenue**

  ```
  SUM(IF  [EOM Club (group)]!= 'Bronze' THEN [Revenue Total] END)
  ```

- **Color : % from Total Cash Out**

  ```
  '% Club Cash Out from eToro'
  ```

- **Color : % from Total Deposit**

  ```
  '% Club Deposits from eToro'
  ```

- **Color : % from Total Revenue**

  ```
  '% of Club Revenue from eToro'
  ```

- **Exclude Reporting Month**

  ```
  [Active Date] <[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Previous Reporting Month**

  ```
  [Active Date] = DATEADD('month',-1,[Reporting Month])
  ```

- **RegionFilter**

  ```
  IF [New Marketing Region] = [Region] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Region] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **RegulationFilter **

  ```
  IF  [EOM Regulation]= [Regulation] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Regulation] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **Reporting Month**

  ```
  [Active Date] = [Reporting Month]
  and [Active Date] < DATETRUNC('month',TODAY())
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe long**

  ```
  [Active Date]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Long]+1,[Reporting Month])
  and [Active Date]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe long (copy)**

  ```
  [Active Date]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Long]+1,[Reporting Month])
  and [Active Date]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe Short**

  ```
  [Active Date]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Short],[Reporting Month])
  and [Active Date]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Total Cash Out**

  ```
  SUM([Total Cashouts])
  ```

- **Total Deposit**

  ```
  SUM([Total Deposits])
  ```

- **Total Revenue**

  ```
  SUM([Revenue Total])
  ```

- **Users**

  ```
  COUNT([CID])
  ```

#### Datasource: Club Members

- **% Opt-In from Eligible**

  ```
  SUM([Is Opt In Interest])/SUM([IsOpt-In Eligible])
  ```

- **ActiveDate**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('month',[Date])
  ```

- **Club Members**

  ```
  COUNTD([CID])
  ```

- **Club Region**

  ```
  IF [Name (Dim Country)] IN ('Denmark','Finland','Netherlands','Norway','Sweden') THEN 'Nordic'
  ELSEIF  [Name (Dim Country)] IN ('Poland','Romania','Slovakia','Slovenia','Czech Republic') THEN 'EE'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('South & Central America','Spain') THEN 'Spanish'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('Other Asia','China') THEN 'SEA'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('Arabic Other','Arabic GCC') THEN 'Arabic'
  ELSEIF [Region] IN ('French','German','Italian','UK','USA','Australia') THEN [Region]
  ELSE 'ROW' END
  ```

- **Club Tier**

  ```
  [Name]
  ```

- **Club Tier Realized Equity**

  ```
  IF [Realized Equity] >=250000 THEN 'Diamond'
      ELSEIF [Realized Equity] >=50000 THEN 'Platinum Plus'
          ELSEIF [Realized Equity] >=25000 THEN 'Platinum'
              ELSEIF [Realized Equity] >=10000 THEN 'Gold'
                  ELSEIF [Realized Equity] >=5000 THEN 'Silver'
                      ELSE 'Bronze' END
  ```

- **Club Tier Realized Equity Club**

  ```
  IF [Realized Equity Club] >=250000 THEN 'Diamond'
      ELSEIF [Realized Equity Club] >=50000 THEN 'Platinum Plus'
          ELSEIF [Realized Equity Club] >=25000 THEN 'Platinum'
              ELSEIF [Realized Equity Club] >=10000 THEN 'Gold'
                  ELSEIF [Realized Equity Club] >=5000 THEN 'Silver'
                      ELSE 'Bronze' END
  ```

- **Cub Tier - First From**

  ```
  { FIXED [CID]: MIN([Sort (Dim PlayerLevel)])}
  ```

- **Cub Tier - Last Upgrade**

  ```
  { FIXED [CID]: MAX([Sort])}
  ```

- **Current Club Tier**

  ```
  IF [Is Downgrade] = 1 THEN [Name (Dim PlayerLevel)] ELSE [Club Tier] END
  ```

- **Is FirstTime Club**

  ```
  [Is FTC]
  ```

- **Is InterestPaid**

  ```
  IF [InterestPaid]>0 THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **IsOpt-In Eligible**

  ```
  IF [Regulation ID] in (1,2,4,10) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
  ```

- **RegionFilter**

  ```
  IF [Marketing Region Manual Name] = [Region] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Region] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **RegulationFilter**

  ```
  IF [Regulation] = [Regulation] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Regulation] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **Reporting Month**

  ```
  [ActiveDate] = [Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe long**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Long]+1,[Reporting Month])
  and [ActiveDate]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe Short**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Short],[Reporting Month])
  and [ActiveDate]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

#### Datasource: Conversion for upgrade

- **%Conversion to upgrade**

  ```
  [Upgraded]/[CID]
  ```

- **County color**

  ```
  { FIXED [ActiveDate],[NewMarketingRegion] : SUM([Upgraded])}
  /{ FIXED [ActiveDate],[NewMarketingRegion] : COUNT([CID])}
  ```

- **RegionFilter**

  ```
  IF [NewMarketingRegion] = [Region] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Region] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

  ```
  [ActiveDate]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Long]+1,[Reporting Month])
  and [ActiveDate]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

- **%Conversion to upgrade**

  ```
  [Upgraded]/[CID]
  ```

- **County color**

  ```
  { FIXED [ActiveDate],[NewMarketingRegion] : SUM([Upgraded])}
  /{ FIXED [ActiveDate],[NewMarketingRegion] : COUNT([CID])}
  ```

- **RegionFilter**

  ```
  IF [NewMarketingRegion] = [Region] THEN 1 
   ELSEIF [Region] = 'All' THEN 1 else 0 END
  ```

- **Reporting Month Timeframe long**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]>=  DATEADD('month',-[Timeframe Long]+1,[Reporting Month])
  and [ActiveDate]<=[Reporting Month]
  ```

### Workbook: Monthly MIMO Report

#### Datasource: Custom SQL Query (BI_DB)

- **%change co/deposit ratio prev month**

  ```
  [CO/Deposits Ratio Last Month]-[CO/Deposits Ratio Prev Month]
  ```

- **%change net deposit from prev month **

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth]=TRUE then [NetDeposits] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth]=TRUE then [NetDeposits] else null end)-1
  ```

- **%Change Prev Month - Avg Cashout**

  ```
  [Avg.Cashouts Last Month]/[Avg.Cashouts Prev Month ]-1
  ```

- **%Change Prev Month - Avg Deposit**

  ```
  [Avg.Deposit Last Month]/[Avg.Deposit Prev Month]-1
  ```

- **%change total cashouts from prev month **

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)-1
  ```

- **%change total deposits from prev month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **%change unique cashouts prev month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)-1
  ```

- **%change unique depositors prev month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change Avg.CO**

  ```
  [Avg.Cashouts Last Month]/[Avg.Cashouts 5 Months]-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change Avg.Deposit**

  ```
  [Avg.Deposit Last Month]/[Avg.Deposits 5 Months ]-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change Net Deposit**

  ```
  [Last MOnth Net Deposits]/[Net Deposits Last 5 Months]-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change total CO**

  ```
  [Last Month CO]/[Total CO Last 5 Months (Avg) ]-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change total co/dep ratio**

  ```
  [CO/Deposits Ratio Last Month]-[CO/Dep ratio last 5 month]
  ```

- **5 Months- %change total deposits**

  ```
  [TotalDeposits LastMonth]/[Total Deposit Last 5 Months (Avg)]-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change unique cashouts**

  ```
  [Last Month Unique Cashouts]/[Unique Cashouts 5 Months ]-1
  ```

- **5 Months- %change unique depositors**

  ```
  [Last Month Unique Depositors]/[Unique Depositors 5 Months]-1
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts**

  ```
  sum([TotalCashouts])/sum([Unique Cashouts])
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts 5 Months**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast5Month] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/sum(if [IsLast5Month] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts Last Month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Cashouts Prev Month **

  ```
  sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit**

  ```
  sum([TotalDeposits])/sum([Unique Depositors])
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit Last Month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)/sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Deposit Prev Month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)/sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)
  ```

- **Avg.Deposits 5 Months **

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast5Month] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)/sum(if [IsLast5Month] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)
  ```

- **Club**

  ```
  if [EOM_Club] in ('LowBronze','HighBronze') then 'Bronze' else [EOM_Club] END
  ```

- **CO/Dep ratio last 5 month**

  ```
  [Total CO Last 5 Months (Avg) ]/[Total Deposit Last 5 Months (Avg)]
  ```

- **CO/Deposit Ratio (CID)**

  ```
  sum([Unique Cashouts])/sum([Unique Depositors])
  ```

- **CO/Deposits Ratio**

  ```
  SUM([TotalCashouts])/ SUM([TotalDeposits])
  ```

- **CO/Deposits Ratio Last Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/ SUM(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **CO/Deposits Ratio Prev Month**

  ```
  SUM(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/ SUM(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **IsLast5Month**

  ```
  [ActiveDate]<DATEADD('month',-2,TODAY())
  and [ActiveDate]>DATEADD('month',-7,TODAY())
  ```

- **IsLastMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[ActiveDate],today())=1 then TRUE END
  ```

- **IsPreviousMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[ActiveDate],today())=2 then TRUE END
  ```

- **IsThisMonth**

  ```
  if datediff('month',[ActiveDate],today())=0 then TRUE END
  ```

- **Last Month CO**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)
  ```

- **Last MOnth Net Deposits**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth]=TRUE then [NetDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **Last Month Unique Cashouts**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)
  ```

- **Last Month Unique Depositors**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)
  ```

- **Net Deposits Last 5 Months**

  ```
  [Total Deposit Last 5 Months (Avg)]-[Total CO Last 5 Months (Avg) ]
  ```

- **Seniority Groups**

  ```
  IF [Seniority_FundedNew] <= 3 THEN "0-3"
  ELSEIF [Seniority_FundedNew] > 3 and [Seniority_FundedNew] <= 6 THEN "4-6"
  ELSEIF [Seniority_FundedNew] > 6 and [Seniority_FundedNew] <= 12 THEN "7-12"
  ELSEIF [Seniority_FundedNew] > 12 and [Seniority_FundedNew]<=18   THEN "12-18"
  ELSEIF [Seniority_FundedNew] > 18 and [Seniority_FundedNew]<=24   THEN "18-24"
  ELSEIF [Seniority_FundedNew] > 24 and [Seniority_FundedNew]<=36   THEN "24-36"
  ELSEIF [Seniority_FundedNew] > 36   THEN "36+"
  ELSE "Not Funded" END
  ```

- **Total CO Last 5 Months (Avg) **

  ```
  sum (if [IsLast5Month] then [TotalCashouts] else null end)/5
  ```

- **Total Deposit Last 5 Months (Avg)**

  ```
  sum (if [IsLast5Month] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)/5
  ```

- **TotalDeposits LastMonth**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLastMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **TotalDeposits Prev Month**

  ```
  sum(if [IsPreviousMonth] then [TotalDeposits] else null end)
  ```

- **Unique Cashouts 5 Months **

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast5Month] then [Unique Cashouts] else null end)/5
  ```

- **Unique Depositors 5 Months**

  ```
  sum(if [IsLast5Month] then [Unique Depositors] else null end)/5
  ```

### Workbook: Test Jan

#### Datasource: All KPIs

- ** Deposit Calculation**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: 
     MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND 
             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') 
         THEN [Actual Deposit+IBAN ]
     END) 
  }
  ```

- **%Achievement Trigger**

  ```
  (COUNTD([Id])-COUNTD([Expierd]))/COUNTD([Id])
  ```

- **Achievement in % **

  ```
  IF  [Gross deposit + Cashout Achievement ]/SUM([Deposit Target ])>2 THEN 2 ELSE  [Gross deposit + Cashout Achievement ]/SUM([Deposit Target ]) END
  ```

- **Action Date**

  ```
  DATETRUNC('day', [Date (Custom SQL Query3)])
  ```

- **Active Open Link**

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/AccountManagerTargets_17102292560510/ActiveOpenByCID?:iid=1'
  ```

  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/Activitiesreports/ActivitiesAMsSAMsByDay?:iid=1'
  ```

- **Activities By Region Link **

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/Activitiesreports/ActivitiesByRegion?:iid=2'
  ```

- **ActivitiesAMsSAMs Link**

  ```
  'https://reports.etorocorp.com/#/views/Activitiesreports/ActivitiesAMsSAMs'
  ```

- **Actual Cashout**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond Cashout] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Cashout] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalCashouts_ThisMonth (Custom SQL Query7)]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

  ```

    ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Deposit**

  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond Deposit]

  ```

  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Contacted**

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[Contacted]: MAX(IF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Diamond' AND [Contacted]=1 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [Diamond open IBAM] 
  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=1  THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=1 and [Club (Custom SQL Query7)] in ('Platinum Plus', 'Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **Actual Open IBAN Not Contacted **

  ```

  ELSEIF  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] and [region] = 'UK - Platinum Plus' AND [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' and [Contacted]=0 THEN [Platinum Plus Open IBAN] 
  ELSEIF [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [Contacted]=0 and [type_of_kpi] = 'Deposit' THEN [TotalOpenfromIBAN_ThisMonth]  ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

- **AM Deposit Achievement in %  **

  ```
  IF SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) >1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE  SUM([Actual Deposit AM])/SUM([Contacted Deposit Target  ]) END
  ```

- **AM Engagement Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Engagement' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Achievement**

  ```
  if [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ])>1.25 THEN 1.25 ELSE [AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation ]/SUM([AM MoneyIn Target ]) END
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn final amount for calculation **

  ```
  SUM([Actual MoneyIn (copy)_1240178748756172801])+IFNULL( SUM([Invested in campaign with contact  (copy)_783626348631248896])*0.2,0)
  ```

- **AM MoneyIn Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn AM' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **AM Total Achievement**

  ```
  IF ISNULL([QC Achievement %]) THEN 
      IF [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ] > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]
      END
  ELSE 
      IF ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 > 1.25 THEN 
          1.25 
      ELSE 
          ([QC Achievement %] + [AM Upgrade Achievement in %  ]) / 2 
      END
  END
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Achievement in %  **

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[Date],[region],[Contact Upgrade],[IsUpgrade]:
  IF MIN([Contact Upgrade]) = 1 AND MIN([IsUpgrade]) = 1 THEN
          IF COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) >1.5 THEN 1.5 
  ELSE  COUNT([CID])/SUM([AM Upgrade Target ]) END
  END}
  ```

- **AM Upgrade Target **

  ```
  { FIXED [Date],[Account Manager],[type_of_kpi],[region]: MAX(IF [type_of_kpi] = 'Upgrade from Platinum' THEN [target] END)}
  ```

- **Amount dep**

  ```
  { FIXED  [RealCID], [Action Date],[Account Manager],[ActionType (Custom SQL Query3)],[AccountType]:SUM([Amount])}
  ```

- **Amount To Upgrade**

  ```
  50000 - [ClubEquity]
  ```

- **AO Achievement**

  ```
  IF  [AO Actual Ratio]<=max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy 2)**

  ```
  IF  INT([AO Actual Ratio])<=INT(max([AO Portfolio benchmark] )) THEN [AO Actual Ratio]
  ELSEIF[AO Actual Ratio]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([AO Actual Ratio]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Achievement (copy)**

  ```
  IF  [RM AO old]<max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ) THEN 0.25
  ELSEIF [RM AO old]/max([AO Target])>1.25 THEN 1.25
  ELSEIF 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5>1.25 THEN 1.25 
  ELSE 0.5 * ([RM AO old]-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))/(max([AO Target])-max([AO Portfolio benchmark] ))+0.5
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **AO Actual Ratio (copy)**

  ```
  IF  ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF ATTR([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **AO Diamond **

  { FIXED [Account Manager],[ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn' THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }

- **AO Portfolio benchmark (copy)**

  ```
  ((sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [ActiveDate],[region],[type_of_kpi],[EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate]THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  ```

  ```

- **Cash out ratio benchmark  cat**

  ```
  if SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) })>0.9 THEN 0.9 ELSE
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Cashout  ]+[Total Close from IBAN]  END) })/
  SUM({FIXED [Date],[type_of_kpi],[region],[Club (Custom SQL Query7)],[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[AccountManager (Custom SQL Query7)]: MAX(IF DATEDIFF('month',[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)],[Date])<=6 AND  [Date]>[ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query7)] AND [type_of_kpi] in('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') THEN [Total Deposit ]+[Total Open from IBAN]  END) }) END
  ```

             [type_of_kpi] IN ('InternalDeposit', 'Deposit') 
         THEN [Actual Cashout+IBAN] 
     END) 
  }

  ```

  ELSE (sum ( [Actual Cashout+IBAN])/ ([final without *]) ) END
  ```

  ```

- **Nt Deposit *13.33%**

  ```
  IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]*13.33/100>0.1333 then 0.1333 else [RM Net Deposit Achievement]*13.33/100 END
  ```

- **Number Of Attempted Phone**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)], [ActionType], [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID] : 
  MAX(IF [ActionType] = 'Contacted__c' THEN [NumberOfCall (Custom SQL Query2)] ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

  ```

  ```

- **PI Meeting Achievement**

  ```
  IF  MAX([PI Meeting Final])/MAX([PI Meeting Target ])>1 THEN 1 ELSE MAX([PI Meeting Final])/MAX([PI Meeting Target ]) end
  ```

- **QC Achievement %**

  ```
  { FIXED [Account Manager],[Date],[region]:
  IF [AVG QC]>= 90 AND [AVG QC] <= 100 THEN 1
      ELSEIF  [AVG QC] >= 80 AND [AVG QC] <= 89 THEN 0.75
      ELSEIF [AVG QC] >= 70 AND [AVG QC] <= 79 THEN 0.5
      ELSEIF [AVG QC] >= 1 AND [AVG QC] <= 69 THEN 0
  
  END}
  ```

- **Ratio AO Diamond**

  ```

  ```

- **Region Without Individual**

  ```
  IF [region] IN ('Harry Charitou','Vyacheslav Zagalski') THEN 'UK - Platinum Plus' ELSE [region] END
  ```

  ```

  ```

- **RM AM 30%**

  ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]*0.15+[RM AM QC achievemnt]*0.15 END
  ```

  ```

- **RM AO old**

  ```
  IF  MAX([region]) = 'UK - Diamond' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  ELSEIF MAX([region]) = 'UK - Platinum Plus' THEN 
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })
  
  ELSE 
  ((sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Diamond') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*1 +
  (sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [ActiveOpenWOAirdropManual (Custom SQL Query8)] END) })/
  sum ({ FIXED [region],[Account Manager],[CalendarYearQtr],[Date]: MAX(IF [EOM_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] in ('Platinum Plus') and [type_of_kpi] = 'MoneyIn'  and [Date] = [ActiveDate] THEN [Total_In_Club (Custom SQL Query8)] END) }))*9
  )/10
  END
  ```

- **RM Club Member Achievement **

  ```
  IF  MAX([ClubMember])>=SUM([RM Club Member Target]) THEN MAX([ClubMember])/SUM([RM Club Member Target]) 
  ELSEIF (MAX([ClubMember])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))/(SUM([RM Club Member Target])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))>1 THEN 1 ELSE (MAX([ClubMember])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ]))/(SUM([RM Club Member Target])-MAX([ClubMemberLastQ])) END
  ```

  )
  END
  }

- **Total Achievement **

  ```
  IF ([trustpilot ]>=SUM([Trustpilot Target  ])) THEN
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1.25 THEN 1.25 
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  ELSE 
      IF ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3 >1 THEN 1
      ELSE ([Achievement in % ] + [MoneyIn Achievement ] + [%Achievement Trigger])/3  END
  end
  ```

- **Total RM Achievement**

  ```
  (IF  [RM Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Deposit Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM Trigger Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Trigger Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM MoneyIn Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM MoneyIn Achievement ] END +
  IF  [RM AM Upgrade Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM Upgrade Achievement] END +
  IF  [RM AM QC achievemnt]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM AM QC achievemnt] END
  ) * 0.1
  +
  (IF  [RM Net Deposit Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSEif [RM Net Deposit Achievement]<0 THEN 0 ELSE [RM Net Deposit Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Revenue Achievement]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Revenue Achievement]END +
  IF  [RM Club Member Achievement ]>1 THEN 1 ELSE [RM Club Member Achievement ]END 
  )*40/3/100
  ```

  ```
  ([RM Deposit Achievement]+[RM Trigger Achievement]+[RM MoneyIn Achievement ]+[RM AM Upgrade Achievement]+[RM AM QC achievemnt]+[RM AM Engagement Achievement])*0.1
  + ([RM Net Deposit Achievement]+[RM Revenue Achievement]+[RM Club Member Achievement ])*40/3/100
  ```

- **Working Day**

  ```
  { FIXED  [AccountManagerID (Custom SQL Query10)],  [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)],[Date (Custom SQL Query10)],[ID],[Date] : 
  MAX(IF  
  ([NumOfCall]>2 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('CompletedPhone'))
  or ([NumOfCall]>7 AND  [Date] = [ActiveDate (Custom SQL Query10)] and [ActionType] IN ('InboundEmail'))
    THEN 1 ELSE NULL end) }
  ```

### Workbook: UK Finance General Dashboard

#### Datasource: active users

- **Active CID**

  ```
  { FIXED [CID],[Period]:MAX([Active (Opened or Held a position during Period])}
  ```

- **Funded User **

  ```
  { FIXED [CID],[Period]:MAX([Funded User End Of Period])}
  ```

- **Period**

  ```
  if [Level Of Detail]='Monthly' then 
  DATEADD('day',-1,(DATEADD('month',1,DATETRUNC('month',[Date]))))
  else DATEADD('day',-1,DATEADD('year',1,DATETRUNC('year',[Date])))
  end
  ```

  ```

  [FullCommissionOnCloseAdjustment]+[FullCommissions]
  ```

  ```

  else DATEADD('day',-1,DATEADD('year',1,DATETRUNC('year',[MonthEnding])))
  end
  ```
